        <p>Government of India is taking all necessary steps to ensure that we are prepared well to face the challenge and threat posed by the growing pandemic of COVID-19 the Corona Virus. With active support of the people of India, we have been able to contain the spread of the Virus in our country. The most important factor in preventing the spread of the Virus locally is to empower the citizens with the right information and taking precautions as per the advisories being issued by Ministry of Health & Family Welfare.</p>

            <h2>Myth Busters</h2>
            <div class="myth_blockquote">
                <h3>There is a lot of false information around. These are the facts.</h3>
                <p> People of all ages CAN be infected by the coronavirus. Older people, and people with pre-existing medical conditions (such as <strong>asthma</strong>, <strong>diabetes</strong>, <strong>heart</strong> disease) appear to be more vulnerable to becoming severely ill with the virus.</p>

    <!--Myth data start-->
    <div class="overlay"></div>
    <div id="myth_model"><i class="closePop"></i>
        <h2>Myth-Busters <span>These are the facts.</span></h2>
        <ul class="myth_list">
            <li>
                <div class="myth_icon"><img src="https://www.mygov.in/sites/all/themes/mygov/images/covid/dis_type_1.png" alt=""></div>
                <div class="myth_text">Cold weather and snow CANNOT kill the CoronaVirus .</div>
            </li>
            <li>
                <div class="myth_icon"><img src="https://www.mygov.in/sites/all/themes/mygov/images/covid/dis_type_2.png" alt=""></div>
                <div class="myth_text">Hand dryers are NOT effective in killing the coronavirus.</div>
            </li>
            <li>
                <div class="myth_icon"><img src="https://www.mygov.in/sites/all/themes/mygov/images/covid/dis_type_3.png" alt=""></div>
                <div class="myth_text">There is NO evidence that regularly rinsing the nose with saline has protected people from infection with the coronavirus. </div>
            </li>
            <li>
                <div class="myth_icon"><img src="https://www.mygov.in/sites/all/themes/mygov/images/covid/dis_type_4.png" alt=""></div>
                <div class="myth_text">The coronavirus CAN be transmitted in areas with hot and humid climates.</div>
            </li>
            <li>
                <div class="myth_icon"><img src="https://www.mygov.in/sites/all/themes/mygov/images/covid/dis_type_5.png" alt=""></div>
                <div class="myth_text">Ultraviolet light SHOULD NOT be used for sterilization and can cause skin irritation.</div>
            </li>
            <li>
                <div class="myth_icon"><img src="https://www.mygov.in/sites/all/themes/mygov/images/covid/dis_type_6.png" alt=""></div>
                <div class="myth_text">Garlic is healthy but there is NO evidence from the current outbreak that eating garlic has protected people from the coronavirus.</div>
            </li>
            <li>
                <div class="myth_icon"><img src="https://www.mygov.in/sites/all/themes/mygov/images/covid/dis_type_7.png" alt=""></div>
                <div class="myth_text">The coronavirus CANNOT be transmitted through mosquito bites.</div>
            </li>
            <li>
                <div class="myth_icon"><img src="https://www.mygov.in/sites/all/themes/mygov/images/covid/dis_type_8.png" alt=""></div>
                <div class="myth_text">Thermal scanners CAN detect if people have a fever but CANNOT detect whether or not someone has the coronavirus.</div>
            </li>
            <li>
                <div class="myth_icon"><img src="https://www.mygov.in/sites/all/themes/mygov/images/covid/dis_type_9.png" alt=""></div>
                <div class="myth_text">Antibiotics DO NOT work against viruses, antibiotics only work against bacteria.</div>
            </li>
            <li>
                <div class="myth_icon"><img src="https://www.mygov.in/sites/all/themes/mygov/images/covid/dis_type_10.png" alt=""></div>
                <div class="myth_text">There is NO evidence that companion animals/pets such as dogs or cats can transmit the coronavirus.</div>
            </li>
            <li>
                <div class="myth_icon"><img src="https://www.mygov.in/sites/all/themes/mygov/images/covid/dis_type_11.png" alt=""></div>
                <div class="myth_text">Spraying alcohol or chlorine all over your body WILL NOT kill viruses that have already entered your body.</div>
            </li>
            <li>
                <div class="myth_icon"><img src="https://www.mygov.in/sites/all/themes/mygov/images/covid/dis_type_13.png" alt=""></div>
                <div class="myth_text">To date, there is NO specific medicine recommended to prevent or treat the coronavirus.</div>
            </li>
            <li>
                <div class="myth_icon"><img src="https://www.mygov.in/sites/all/themes/mygov/images/covid/dis_type_14.png" alt=""></div>
                <div class="myth_text">Taking a hot bath DOES NOT prevent the coronavirus.</div>
            </li>
            <li>
                <div class="myth_icon"><img src="https://www.mygov.in/sites/all/themes/mygov/images/covid/dis_type_15.png" alt=""></div>
                <div class="myth_text">Vaccines against pneumonia, such as pneumococcal vaccine and Haemophilus influenzae type b (Hib) vaccine, DO NOT provide protection against the coronavirus.</div>
            </li>
        </ul>
        <div class="dis_note"><i></i> Note : Content is Sourced from <a href="https://www.who.int" target="_blank">World Health Organization</a> </div>
    </div>
    <!--Myth data end-->
